/-->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"featured-area\"><div class=\"featured-area-inner\"><figure class=\"single-featured-image\"><img width=\"780\" height=\"470\" src=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/780x470-1.png\" class=\"attachment-jannah-image-post size-jannah-image-post wp-post-image\" alt=\"365Scores monkey Predictions Cup game\" data-main-img=\"1\" decoding=\"async\" fetchpriority=\"high\" srcset=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/780x470-1.png 780w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/780x470-1-300x181.png 300w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/780x470-1-768x463.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<figcaption class=\"single-caption-text\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"tie-icon-camera\" aria-hidden=\"true\"></span> 365Scores Predictions Cup game\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</figcaption>\n\t\t\t\t\t</figure></div></div>\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content entry clearfix\">\n\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\n<p>&nbsp;Exciting news for football fans! As the world’s biggest sporting event heads to North America, 365Scores has officially launched its highly anticipated<a href=\"https://www.365scores.com/en-us\"> </a><a href=\"https://www.365scores.com/en-us/football/league/fifa-world-cup-5930\">FIFA World Cup 2026</a> predictor game. With 48 teams competing across the<a href=\"https://www.365scores.com/en-us/football/team/usa-2389\"> United States</a>, Canada, and Mexico, this is your chance to join an exhilarating match prediction contest.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Compete against your friends, family, and other fans globally to see who can accurately predict the outcomes of the biggest matches in international football. Don’t miss out on this opportunity to showcase your football knowledge and win ultimate bragging rights. Join now and get ready for an unforgettable summer tournament!</p>\n\n\n\n<p><em>(In the <a href=\"https://www.365scores.com/en-us\">365Scores</a> app, click on </em><strong><em>Predictions Cup</em></strong><em> button to get started!)</em></p>\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n<figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img decoding=\"async\" width=\"540\" height=\"933\" src=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-55.png\" alt=\"Predictions Cup \" class=\"wp-image-18761\" srcset=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-55.png 540w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-55-174x300.png 174w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 540px) 100vw, 540px\"><figcaption class=\"wp-element-caption\">(Via 365Scores)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity\">\n\n\n\n<h3 class=\"wp-block-heading\"><strong>How to play the 365Scores Predictions Cup?</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>To join a league, simply use the invite link from your friends or create your own inside the app or web. You will be able to create custom leagues with your mates and compete to see who truly has the best football IQ. You’ll also automatically be entered into the Global World League. Imagine if you won it all against millions of other fans!</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 class=\"wp-block-heading\"><strong>The Rules &amp; Point System</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Get ready for the ultimate football prediction challenge. Registration is open now and will close just before the knockout rounds heat up. Here is how you can rack up your score:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Pre-Tournament Guesses:</strong></p>\n\n\n\n<ul class=\"wp-block-list\">\n<li><strong>Tournament Winner:</strong> 12 points</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Top Scorer:</strong> 12 points</li>\n</ul>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>Match-by-Match Predictions:</strong> Earn points for guessing the correct match result (win/lose/draw) and the exact scoreline:</p><div class=\"stream-item stream-item-in-post stream-item-inline-post aligncenter\"><div class=\"stream-item-size\" style=\"\"><div data-aaad=\"true\" data-aa-adunit=\"/183758631/Banner_Moblie_MagazineEN_336x280_Article_Mid1\" data-aa-lazy-loaded=\"true\" data-status=\"skipped\" id=\"ea2a1c72-0d9d-4450-91af-e50c164499ef\" data-aa-device=\"[&quot;mobile&quot;]\" data-aa-sizes=\"[[336,280],[300,600],[300,250],[300,100],[300,50],[250,250],[200,200],[160,600],[120,600]]\" data-aa-rich-media-format=\"{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;flyingCarpet&quot;,&quot;options&quot;:{&quot;showLabel&quot;:&quot;false&quot;}}\" data-aa-refresh-viewable=\"30\" data-aa-additional-non-h-b-sizes=\"[&quot;fluid&quot;]\"></div>\n<div data-aaad=\"true\" data-aa-adunit=\"/183758631/Banner_Desktop_MagazineEN_728x90_Article_Mid1\" data-aa-lazy-loaded=\"true\" data-status=\"lazyLoaded\" id=\"d0f2c972-5daa-4bc4-a78d-c217a0a4c1dc\" data-aa-device=\"[&quot;desktop&quot;]\" data-aa-sizes=\"[[728,90],[468,60]]\" data-aa-refresh-viewable=\"30\" data-aa-additional-non-h-b-sizes=\"[&quot;fluid&quot;]\"></div></div></div>\n\n\n\n<ul class=\"wp-block-list\">\n<li><strong>Group Stages:</strong> 1 point (correct result) / 3 points (exact score)</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Round of 32 &amp; Round of 16:</strong> 2 points / 5 points</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Quarterfinals:</strong> 4 points / 8 points</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Semifinals &amp; Third place:</strong> 5 points / 10 points</li>\n\n\n\n<li><strong>Final:</strong> 8 points / 15 points</li>\n</ul>\n\n\n\n<p>The 365Scores Predictions Cup is fantastic fun, but the stakes are high. We chose <a href=\"https://www.365scores.com/en-us/football/team/england-5054\">England</a> to finally bring it home this time around—but who will you pick?</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n<figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"473\" height=\"744\" src=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-44.png\" alt=\"Predictions Cup rules\" class=\"wp-image-18706\" srcset=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-44.png 473w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/image-44-191x300.png 191w\" sizes=\"auto, (max-width: 473px) 100vw, 473px\"></figure></div>\n\n\n<h3 class=\"wp-block-heading\"><strong>Important Details to Remember</strong></h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Predictions can be made or changed right up until kick-off for each specific match, while your overall tournament winner and top scorer guesses can be altered until the very first match of the World Cup begins.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Final scores for predictions are determined after 90 minutes in the group stages, and after 120 minutes in the knockout stages (excluding penalty shootouts). <strong>Forgot to make a pick?</strong> If no prediction is entered for a match, our virtual monkey will randomly guess for you!</p>\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n<figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img loading=\"lazy\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"512\" height=\"1024\" src=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Phone_Screen-04-512x1024.png\" alt=\"Predictions Cup, top scorer \" class=\"wp-image-18763\" srcset=\"https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Phone_Screen-04-512x1024.png 512w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Phone_Screen-04-150x300.png 150w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Phone_Screen-04-768x1536.png 768w, https://www.365scores.com/news/wp-content/uploads/2026/05/Phone_Screen-04-scaled.png 1024w\" sizes=\"auto, (max-width: 512px) 100vw, 512px\"><figcaption class=\"wp-element-caption\">(Via 365Scores)</figcaption></figure></div>\n\n\n<p>Real-time updates will keep you in the loop as goals fly in across the Americas. Please note that late registrants won’t receive points for past games. In the event of a tie at the end of the tournament, tiebreakers will be decided by: the number of exact scores, correct results, goals scored by your chosen top scorer, your tournament winner guess, and finally, your registration time.</p><div class=\"stream-item stream-item-in-post stream-item-inline-post aligncenter\"><div class=\"stream-item-size\" style=\"\"><div data-aaad=\"true\"
